Math.imul =  function (a, b) {
  var ah = (a >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var al = a & 0xffff;
  var bh = (b >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var bl = b & 0xffff;
  return ((al * bl) + (((ah * bl + al * bh) << 16) >>> 0) | 0);
};

Math.imul =  function (a, b) {
  var ah = (a >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var al = a & 0xffff;
  var bh = (b >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var bl = b & 0xffff;
  return ((al * bl) + (((ah * bl + al * bh) << 16) >>> 0) | 0);
};

Math.imul =  function (a, b) {
  var ah = (a >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var al = a & 0xffff;
  var bh = (b >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var bl = b & 0xffff;
  return ((al * bl) + (((ah * bl + al * bh) << 16) >>> 0) | 0);
};

Math.imul =  function (a, b) {
  var ah = (a >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var al = a & 0xffff;
  var bh = (b >>> 16) & 0xffff;
  var bl = b & 0xffff;
  return ((al * bl) + (((ah * bl + al * bh) << 16) >>> 0) | 0);
};
